          <h2 class="date-header">
           <span>
            26 enero 2017
           </span>
          </h2>
          <div class="date-posts">
           <div class="post-outer">
            <div class="post hentry">
             <div class="post-cover">
              <a name="2760627899196294952">
              </a>
              <div class="bposttitle">
               <h2 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.securitybydefault.com/2017/01/utilizando-la-esteganografia-para-salir.html">
                 Utilizando la esteganografía para salir del radar de control (I)
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="postmeta">
                <span class="metaauthor">
                 Autor:  
                             Contribuciones
                </span>
                <span class="clock">
                 26 enero 2017
                             [
                             6:32
                             ]
                </span>
                <span class="tags">
                 <a class="dsq-comment-count comment-link commentslink" href="http://www.securitybydefault.com/2017/01/utilizando-la-esteganografia-para-salir.html#disqus_thread">
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="entry">
               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary2760627899196294952">
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UZsJdeEPrvQ/WIYICiP2W4I/AAAAAAAAALQ/ykqsGzCpVVIURG0C1v93GcmmFxnyoM-5ACLcB/s1600/0.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="300" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UZsJdeEPrvQ/WIYICiP2W4I/AAAAAAAAALQ/ykqsGzCpVVIURG0C1v93GcmmFxnyoM-5ACLcB/s640/0.jpg" width="640"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    Voy a contar una anécdota realizando un hacking ético
                   </span>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                   </span>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    a un banco internacional. El reto propuesto por el jefe de Seguridad, era poder exportar una parte de la BD clientes de la empresa (
                   </span>
                   <span style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    que para hacer la
                    <em style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     PoC
                    </em>
                    , ubicamos un pequeño TXT como objeto
                   </span>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    ), hacia el exterior. Mi ambiente de trabajo era una
                   </span>
                   <em style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    desktop
                   </em>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                   </span>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    perteneciente a un empleado del banco.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 2em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: normal;">
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   Las primeras pruebas que hacemos todos, eran en vano. Los sitios para compartir estaban todos filtrados, los puertos de mi PC no permitían mucha interacción, los correos externos no estaban permitidos y demás. Tratando de buscar una salida a este problema, me encontré con
                   <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    Blogger
                   </strong>
                   (sí, el servicio de
                   <em style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    blogs
                   </em>
                   de Google) y esto me llamó mucho la atención. Todos los servicios de
                   <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    Google
                   </strong>
                   estaban bloqueados, excepto éste. Recuerdo que en ese tiempo tuve mi primer
                   <em style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    blog
                   </em>
                   en esa plataforma.
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 2em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: normal;">
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   Probé autenticarme y accedí. Ya estaba sonriendo, entendiendo donde estaba la posible brecha. El primer intento, fue escribir un nuevo
                   <em style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    post
                   </em>
                   con una foto cualquiera. Le dí a publicar, accedí desde el exterior a mi
                   <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    blog
                   </strong>
                   y ahi estaba la imagen, esperando ansiosamente a ser explotada.
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 2em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: normal;">
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   Tenía dos alternativas:
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <ul style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; list-style-image: initial; list-style-position: initial; margin: 0px 0px 1.5em 3em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                  <li style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                   <div style="text-align: justify;">
                    <span style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     Jugar desde Windows
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">
                     . El comando para este caso era
                    </span>
                    <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     copy
                    </strong>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">
                     : los argumentos a pasarle eran /
                    </span>
                    <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     b
                    </strong>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">
                     (según Microsoft, indica la copia de un archivo
                    </span>
                    <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     binario
                    </strong>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">
                     ), la imagen víctima y luego
                    </span>
                    <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     adicionamos
                    </strong>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">
                     el binario que queremos ocultar,
                    </span>
                    <em style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     zippeado
                    </em>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">
                     . La instrucción quedaría de la siguiente forma:
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <ul style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; list-style: disc; margin: 0px 0px 0px 1.5em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    <li style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-align: justify; vertical-align: baseline;">
                     copy
                     <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                      /b
                     </strong>
                     <span style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">
                      imagen.jpg
                     </span>
                     <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                      +
                     </strong>
                     <span style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">
                      ocultar.zip
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <ul style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; list-style-image: initial; list-style-position: initial; margin: 0px 0px 1.5em 3em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                  <li style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-align: justify; vertical-align: baseline;">
                   <span style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    Jugar desde Linux
                   </span>
                   . Podia hacer lo mismo que en el caso anterior, pero con el comando
                   <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    cat
                   </strong>
                   . Esto no era conveniente, porque dejaba evidencias con conexiones a otros servidores. La mejor decisión era causar la menor cantidad de ruido, levantando muy pocas sospechas.
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 2em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: normal;">
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   Vayamos a lo importante, hagamos una
                   <em style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: inherit; font-weight: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    demo
                   </em>
                   de como fue el ataque:
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-3r8S059UAo0/WIXzKr6mRSI/AAAAAAAAAKw/EYP1urTM0LAET5D_q0RdTa__D9gt1sndQCEw/s1600/1.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="339" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-3r8S059UAo0/WIXzKr6mRSI/AAAAAAAAAKw/EYP1urTM0LAET5D_q0RdTa__D9gt1sndQCEw/s640/1.png" width="640"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     <u>
                      Tenemos nuestros archivos
                     </u>
                     : la imagen y el mensaje secreto.
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <img border="0" height="369" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xI0Y3bE_lOM/WIXzKnrKccI/AAAAAAAAAK0/O4qUd0ZzHfkKeYx-21S-7U0lDpHErzrzQCEw/s640/2.png" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" width="640"/>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     Hacemos el proceso de esteganografía
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xI0Y3bE_lOM/WIXzKnrKccI/AAAAAAAAAK0/O4qUd0ZzHfkKeYx-21S-7U0lDpHErzrzQCEw/s1600/2.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                   Solo resta escribir un
                  </span>
                  <em style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                   post
                  </em>
                  <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                   , subir la imagen y publicarlo:
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MwGJh0qW-Bc/WIXzKyW8D7I/AAAAAAAAAK4/VWd1ENF_ofMAhpJ7iJqTRwa_16WYugfqQCEw/s1600/3.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="408" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MwGJh0qW-Bc/WIXzKyW8D7I/AAAAAAAAAK4/VWd1ENF_ofMAhpJ7iJqTRwa_16WYugfqQCEw/s640/3.png" width="640"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     El post con la imagen, ya está online.
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    Voy a descargarme la imagen con
                   </span>
                   <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    curl
                   </strong>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    y luego con un
                   </span>
                   <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    cat
                   </strong>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    voy a ver su contenido. Si tengo suerte, debería ver el contenido del secreto
                   </span>
                   <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    TXT
                   </strong>
                   <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                    :
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <span style='background-color: white; color: #474747; font-family: "ubuntu" , sans-serif; font-size: 18px;'>
                  <br/>
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LnjSCiXaBV4/WIXzLN3uKMI/AAAAAAAAAK8/sh94Ktxj7wsl2sdQCFsctRDGybhzeI9HwCEw/s1600/4.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="224" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LnjSCiXaBV4/WIXzLN3uKMI/AAAAAAAAAK8/sh94Ktxj7wsl2sdQCFsctRDGybhzeI9HwCEw/s640/4.png" width="640"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     Realizamos la descarga.
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 <br/>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IQoxGCO7gIM/WIXzLL4atJI/AAAAAAAAALA/9UkbDvE80_0amPcQj6AuW6vH69MVVgzSQCEw/s1600/5.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="338" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IQoxGCO7gIM/WIXzLL4atJI/AAAAAAAAALA/9UkbDvE80_0amPcQj6AuW6vH69MVVgzSQCEw/s640/5.png" width="640"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     Vemos el resultado. La palabra
                     <b>
                      SecByDefault
                     </b>
                     estaba oculta en la imagen.
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 2em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: normal;">
                  Podríamos tratar de subir archivos más pesados, con otras extensiones y más importantes que un simple
                  <strong style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                   TXT
                  </strong>
                  , pero eso lo dejamos para una segunda edición.
                 </div>
                 <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #474747; font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 2em; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; word-break: normal;">

         <div class="date-outer">
          <h2 class="date-header">
           <span>
            24 enero 2017
           </span>
          </h2>
          <div class="date-posts">
           <div class="post-outer">
            <div class="post hentry">
             <div class="post-cover">
              <a name="2860256620200766631">
              </a>
              <div class="bposttitle">
               <h2 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.securitybydefault.com/2017/01/entrevista-michael-boelen-el-creador-de.html">
                 Entrevista a Michael Boelen, el creador de Lynis y rkhunter
                </a>
               </h2>
               <div class="postmeta">
                <span class="metaauthor">
                 Autor:  
                             Lorenzo Martínez
                </span>
                <span class="clock">
                 24 enero 2017
                             [
                             6:32
                             ]
                </span>
                <span class="tags">
                 <a class="dsq-comment-count comment-link commentslink" href="http://www.securitybydefault.com/2017/01/entrevista-michael-boelen-el-creador-de.html#disqus_thread">
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="entry">
               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary2860256620200766631">
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zp9BA0ffJvo/WIYG8CoC48I/AAAAAAAAESI/8vlBThcG8pwqjTbHcfCycrwTxa00paOHACLcB/s1600/lynis-screenshot.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="240" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zp9BA0ffJvo/WIYG8CoC48I/AAAAAAAAESI/8vlBThcG8pwqjTbHcfCycrwTxa00paOHACLcB/s320/lynis-screenshot.png" width="320"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   Seguro que a quienes os ha tocado
                   <a href="https://cursos.securizame.com/hardening/hardening-de-sistemas-windows-y-linux-e-infraestructuras#contenido">
                    administrar y securizar máquinas Linux
                   </a>
                   , tenéis a
                   <a href="https://cisofy.com/lynis/">
                    Lynis
                   </a>
                   como una de las herramientas de cabecera, para poder comprobar si os habéis dejado algún agujero por tapar. De hecho, en los inicios de SbD,
                   <a href="http://www.securitybydefault.com/2009/04/lynis-herramienta-de-auditoria-para.html">
                    ya hablábamos sobre esta fantástica herramienta
                   </a>
                   . Pero no Michael no sólo es conocido por Lynis, sino por haber desarrollado tiempo atrás otra herramienta que no puede faltar
                   <a href="https://www.securizame.com/curso-presencial-dfir-y-analisis-forense-en-gnulinux-10-horas-segunda-edicion/">
                    cuando se analiza un incidente de seguridad en Linux, en el que hay una máquina comprometida
                   </a>
                   :
                   <a href="http://rkhunter.sourceforge.net/">
                    RKHunter
                   </a>
                   .
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   Pues hoy os traigo una entrevista al padre de ambas criaturas: Michael Boelen. Holandés y un auténtico experto en Linux. Sin duda una persona de la que aprender, tanto a nivel técnico como por desarrollar Lynis, su proyecto personal, y potenciarlo hasta dedicarse profesionalmente en cuerpo y alma a él.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   La entrevista está en inglés. Pensé en traducirla al español, pero creo que así como lo he hecho en otras, el resultado ha perdido su esencia. Creo que es mejor dejarla en el idioma original y, a no ser que me lo pidáis en los comentarios, la dejamos así.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    SbD - Michael, you are the developer or Lynis, one of the main
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    automated internal auditing tools for GNU/Linux systems. What did make
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <b style="color: #444444; font-family: verdana, sans-serif;">
                   you to start developing this useful tool?
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    Michael Boelen
                   </b>
                   The
  best tools or apps are usually created because of a specific need. I 
 needed a quick way to replace hardening guides (like the CIS benchmarks)
  during my years as a system administrator. Reading the documents simply
  take too much time. And instead of just checking the boxes, I wanted a 
 tool that could test systems on a daily basis and tell me what could be 
 improved.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - I guess you use CIS Benchmarks Guides to adjust the checks they
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <b style="color: #444444; font-family: verdana, sans-serif;">
                   recommend to improve your tool. Which any other sources do you have in mind?
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   That
  is the beauty of a tool like Lynis. It is not limited to one single 
 standard or a set of best practices. Instead, we take the most important
  best practices and combine them into a set of smaller tests. We group 
 them by their focus area, like cryptography, database, mail, web, etc.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - Lynis also has plugins developed by the community, can you talk us
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <b style="color: #444444; font-family: verdana, sans-serif;">
                   about them?
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   The
  plugin system of Lynis extends the normal set of tests. Where normal 
 tests have a clear outcome (good, bad, or could be better), plugins are 
 mainly focused on collecting data. This data could then be used during 
 the tests later on, or their output could be stored in a data report. 
 This data report could then be fed into a SIEM, or a management 
 interface.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - Have you ever thought about creating profiles to be able to measure a
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    system security level depending on the checks that standards like
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <b style="color: #444444; font-family: verdana, sans-serif;">
                   PCI-DSS requires?
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   We
  definitely have. In 2013 we started actually a company (CISOfy) to put 
 more development into Lynis. For companies that have specific 
 requirements (like being compliant with PCI-DSS, HIPAA, or ISO27001), we
  offer a management interface. It leverages the Lynis client tool and 
 adds a web-based interface where all data is stored. And when you have 
 all data in one place, the sum and value of all data from all individual
  systems become much higher. For example finding the questions to how do
  systems compare? Are similar systems also similarly configured? And for
  those with a need of compliance checking, the Enterprise version can do
  a quick scan in this area. Simply add a machine and add a compliance 
 standard, and it will be checked.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - Although Lynis is free, you have this Enterprise version you mentioned. Do you earn
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <b style="color: #444444; font-family: verdana, sans-serif;">
                   your life with this project or do you work somewhere else and Lynis is a
                  </b>
                  <b style="color: #444444; font-family: verdana, sans-serif;">
                   hobby or a complementary job for you?
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   Lynis
  started as a hobby project in 2007. With the business support from 
 CISOfy in 2013, the project has seen a great increase in number of users
  and contributors. I'm full-time involved with business and software 
 development, and that is for us our main stream of income.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                    - There are other tools that says to do the same as Lynis, like Linux Check list
                   </span>
                   <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                    or LSAT. Why is Lynis better than the rest?
                   </span>
                  </b>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   During
  the last 10 years, several tools have seen the light. The big problem 
 with all the tools: they are badly maintained. Still, I see occasionally
  new projects show up and after 6-12 months stop. With Lynis celebrating
  its 10th anniversary, you can be assured that it is well-known and 
 still being maintained. Compared to commercial solutions, Lynis is 
 open-source and vendor-neutral. That is another important aspect of our 
 tool. The last one might be surprising, but Lynis is written in shell 
 script. Not in bash, but bourne shell (/bin/sh). This makes it perfect 
 for people to create their own tests, even if you would use something 
 like Python. Simply fetch the output of your script and embed into your 
 own test. Another benefit is that Lynis runs on AIX, FreeBSD, OpenBSD, 
 Linux, macOS, and others. As long as you have that basic /bin/sh shell 
 available.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - Do you have any tips for people that like to contribute to open source projects?
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   Maybe
  the most important tip is that your involvement with a project could 
 result in the most unbelievable things. Think of finding a job, a 
 mentor, or a friendship. Even if you can't program, you can help making 
 any project better by contributing to the documentation by sharing areas
  that could be improved. Even if you find a small typo, that is already 
 worth sharing.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - For those who can do programming, any tips?
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   If
  you have the gift of being a developer, then I suggest valuing your 
 time. In my opinion, it is better to make one very good tool, than three
  mediocre tools. Focus on easy of use, documentation, design, sane 
 defaults, contributor guidelines and regular program updates. Last but 
 not least, learn the skill of marketing. Even the best open source tools
  need marketing.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - Besides Lynis, are there any projects that you are involved in?
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   People
  might know me from my first big project in the past, named rkhunter 
 (Rootkit Hunter). While I still read about malware, I don't do as much 
 research nowadays. The time of dissecting rootkits is over. Instead, I 
 put in a lot of time to share knowledge regarding Linux security (like 
 'The state of Linux security' --&gt;
                   <a href="https://linux-audit.com/the-state-of-linux-security/">
                    https://linux-audit.com/the-state-of-linux-security/
                   </a>
                   ).
  The blog Linux Audit is one of these places where I share such 
 knowledge. As a technical founder, I find it important to help making 
 the digital world a little bit more secure. By sharing tips and ideas, 
 we can inspire others to take action. Another area includes giving 
 presentations at meetups and conferences. Last year about 10 
 presentations, of which most are available online. Speaking about 
 conferences, I help to organize one in The Netherlands. It is a Dutch 
 UNIX user group (NLUUG), focused on open standards like open source and 
 GNU/Linux. Besides being a board member, I provide my guidance in the 
 program committee to select the right speakers. And another small side 
 project I'm running, is the Twitter handle
                   <a href="http://www.twitter.com/infosec_cfp">
                    @infosec_cfp
                   </a>
                   . It helps 
 security specialists to get involved in call for papers/proposals of any
  security conference they like to speak.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   <b>
                    - If we like to know more about you, what is a good place to look?
                   </b>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="gmail_default" style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span style='color: #444444; font-family: "verdana" , sans-serif;'>
                   Searching my name would be a good start. You will find I'm on Twitter (
                   <a href="http://www.twitter.com/mboelen">
                    @mboelen
                   </a>
                   ), LinkedIn, and have a personal website (
                   <a href="http://michaelboelen.com/">
                    michaelboelen.com
                   </a>
                   ). And don't forget to read the blog [
                   <a href="https://linux-audit.com/">
                    https://linux-audit.com
                   </a>
                   ] :)
                  </span>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <script type="text/javascript">
                 createSummaryAndThumb("summary2860256620200766631");
                </script>
